\hypertarget{interfaceArrayResize__mod_1_1resize}{}\doxysection{Array\+Resize\+\_\+mod\+::resize Interface Reference}
\label{interfaceArrayResize__mod_1_1resize}\index{ArrayResize\_mod::resize@{ArrayResize\_mod::resize}}


Resize an input array to twice its current size or, shrink/expand it to the requested input {\ttfamily size} or to the requested input new lower and upper bounds ({\ttfamily lb, ub}) while keeping the array contents in its original indices in the resized array.  




\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Resize an input array to twice its current size or, shrink/expand it to the requested input {\ttfamily size} or to the requested input new lower and upper bounds ({\ttfamily lb, ub}) while keeping the array contents in its original indices in the resized array. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em Array} & \+: The input/output allocatable array of shape {\ttfamily (\+:)} of either ~\newline
 ~ type {\ttfamily integer} of kind \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceConstants__mod_ae3573d46486b5f1a0a8d5033a9d12879}{IK8}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceConstants__mod_acd3c33e94d12f6e7d7c0ee79b2d6280b}{IK16}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceConstants__mod_ab12a86d74008f0d7f287c3564c3defd9}{IK32}}, or \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceConstants__mod_ad6aaf2f477491dc84e7ebbab3b64694e}{IK64}}, or ~\newline
 ~ type {\ttfamily complex} of kind \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceConstants__mod_ac8b456bd9511bc9a52b4a03bda4b72df}{CK32}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceConstants__mod_aa6ea61256fca0b20db0ec2b90755b9f3}{CK64}}, or \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceConstants__mod_ad3873e1ecc5eb3cf3651f72630cae087}{CK128}}, or ~\newline
 ~ type {\ttfamily real} of kind \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceConstants__mod_aaf5c6c840ed0befe5a37da626c35716f}{RK32}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceConstants__mod_a855643f887b4c787e6542e9e7849680f}{RK64}}, or \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceConstants__mod_aeef7c44b90b75aeeebdef1da504886cb}{RK128}}, or ~\newline
 ~ type {\ttfamily logical} of default kind \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceConstants__mod_a68ac316f10b57be996670bc7c0abed9d}{LK}}, or ~\newline
 ~ type {\ttfamily character} of default kind, or ~\newline
 ~ a scalar assumed-\/length {\ttfamily character} of default kind. ~\newline
 ~ On output, the array will be reallocated to the requested new size or bounds. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em size} & \+: The input scalar {\ttfamily integer} of default kind \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceConstants__mod_a2bf4d6767c9954d3a495d10ab6b538d6}{IK}} representing the new size of the array ({\bfseries{optional}}, default = {\ttfamily 2\+\_\+\+IK}). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em lb} & \+: The input scalar {\ttfamily integer} of default kind \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceConstants__mod_a2bf4d6767c9954d3a495d10ab6b538d6}{IK}} representing the new lower bound of the array after reallocation ~\newline
 ({\bfseries{optional}}, default = {\ttfamily lbound(\+Array)}, it must be present if and only if {\ttfamily ub} is present and {\ttfamily size} is NOT present.). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em ub} & \+: The input scalar {\ttfamily integer} of default kind \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceConstants__mod_a2bf4d6767c9954d3a495d10ab6b538d6}{IK}} representing the new lower bound of the array after reallocation ~\newline
 ({\bfseries{optional}}, default = {\ttfamily lbound(\+Array) + 2$\ast$size(Array) -\/ 1}, must be present if and only if {\ttfamily lb} is also present and {\ttfamily size} is not present).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{fortran_statement}{call} \mbox{\hyperlink{interfaceArrayResize__mod_1_1resize}{resize}}(Array, lb, ub, failed) \textcolor{fortran_comment}{! resize to `Array(lb:ub)`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{!}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
Note that the procedure interface {\ttfamily resize(\+Array, lb, ub)} does not exist when the input {\ttfamily Array} is an {\ttfamily allocatable} scalar {\ttfamily character} because scalar allocatable characters have a fixed lower bound of {\ttfamily 1} that cannot be changed.

When the input argument {\ttfamily size} is present, it must be a non-\/negative integer. ~\newline
 When {\ttfamily lb} and {\ttfamily ub} are present, the condition {\ttfamily lb \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}= ub} must hold. ~\newline
 These conditions are NOT checked for at runtime.

When the specified new array size or bounds are smaller than the originals, the corresponding elements of the old array will be also trimmed from the resized shrunk array.
\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
This procedure is {\ttfamily pure}.
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The sole purpose of this generic interface is to provide a {\bfseries{convenient}} but {\bfseries{fast}} method of resizing allocatable arrays without losing the contents of the array. See \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceArrayResize__mod}{Array\+Resize\+\_\+mod}} for the relevant benchmarks.
\end{DoxyNote}
